--- 帖子 #2013 ---
Thanks skyline for the useful information.

I think the most important thing for those newbies who wants to try firebird is to know that "THERE IS NO MONEY MANAGEMENT BUILD INTO FIREBIRD" and I think that's the killer.  People play big with firebird in the hope to make massive money (but they most likely lost the account).

Take example that you only want to try one pair USD/CHF and get those 40000+PIPs over last 1 and half year, what's the money management you should use?

The drawdown is 4000PIPs, so to be safe, we double it to 8000PIPs that the pips you need to survive the drawdown.  Then say your maximum tolerance risk for your account is 20% drawdown.  If you have US$10000 on "mini" account, then you can only risk $2000 total for that 8000PIPS - that translate to 0.25 lot per trade.  Then those 40000 PIPs profit would translate $10000 profit over last 1 1/2 years which is pretty good.  It is just not matching the "NEWBIE'S EXPECTATION"~~

Then it is the question of "diversification" - people expected that diversification is good and think it can "minimise" the drawdown.  However it is not true for firebird~~ The drawdown are more severe with diversification and believe me it eats all your profit before you ever noticed it.  Therefore if you really want to diversify, you need to reduce the trade size further.

By the way, the backtesting using firebird gives totally different result to the live trade so don't backtest it and think you got the holy grail.

Hope it helps everyone.

--- 帖子 #2015 ---
I totally agree with Skyline.

I also traded this EA live .  You can see my results earlier in this thread.  My risk per trade was 3% and the EA gave great results for several months.  Then I lost most of my account in a few weeks during a strong trend.  I nearly lost the lot but manually bailed out with 50% or my starting balance.  before this period i was up 70%.  So starting with a $1,000 account I ran it up to $1,700, then lost $1,200 in a few weeks.  Not good.

Do not be decieved by good results for a period of time.  30 pips profits with 300 pip losses will nuke your account sooner or later.

I actually tested this EA with great results for a few months then went live thinking I was now on "easy street".  trading this EA went against all that i had come to believe about a good system - but the results were great so it must be good.  Certainly this EA give periods with great results but the inevitable losses will wipe you out.

I have attatched my statement as proof.  Please refer to the first half of the atatched graph.  This is not my only trading account.  I mostly use this one for testing, but it's clear that this EA has some serious problems.

Learn to trade properly.  Do not waste your time and money with this EA.  If you want to trade EAs find one with better stats.  personally i would rather learn to trade the "hard" way.

I gave up on EAs after this one, and am slowly rebuilding my account.

There is no easy way.  I have certainly learnt that lesson after 4 years of trading.  The lessons I have learnt in that time cannot be taught in any other way.

Please do not be deceived by EAs like this.  I don;t know what else to say but I feel for people who get caught by in the trap of what at first appears to be "easy riches" only to lose everything in a matter of time.

I am no expert but I am still here after 4 years trading live.  So I must be doing something right .

Wiz.

--- 帖子 #2019 ---
Open EA in MetaEditor. Find this section and add changes below in Red. You can use any sound .wav file that is in the Sounds folder or find .wav file on internet or make a new .wav file and add to Sounds folder.

Inserted Code if( (myMA*(1+Percent/100))<Bid && Direction!=22 && (Bid>=(LastPrice+(CurrentPipStep*Point)) || MyOrdersTotal()==0) && RVI<0 && dealok)              // modified by Renato
{
OrderSend(Symbol(),OP_SELL,Lots,Bid,slip,Bid+(Stoploss*Point),Bid-(TakeProfit*Point),GetCommentForOrder(),MagicNumber,0,clOpenSell);                              // modified by Renato
[color="red"]PlaySound(Alert.wav);[/color]
ret = 1;
}

// Go LONG -> Only buy if >= 30 pips below previous position entry
if((myMA*(1-Percent/100))>Ask && Direction!=11 && (Ask<=(LastPrice-(CurrentPipStep*Point)) || MyOrdersTotal()==0) && RVI>0 && dealok)  // modified by Renato
{
OrderSend(Symbol(),OP_BUY,Lots,Ask,slip,Ask-(Stoploss*Point),Ask+(TakeProfit*Point),GetCommentForOrder(),MagicNumber,0,clOpenBuy);  // modified by Renato
[color="Red"] PlaySound(Alert.wav);[/color]
ret = 2;
}

--- 帖子 #2021 ---
Having tested v1.0a, I would have to say it was luck based on the market conditions. Be very careful.  In a ranging market you will take profit on a few trades every day with almost no loses.  The float will get large but will not be a problem  because the larger the float the more you gain on a retracement. Then if the market starts trending a bunch of open trades will hit the SL.  Look carefully at your float and count the possible loss if the market trends strongly. I would not recommend trading with real money. As far as trade size  goes it would depend somewhat on how many pairs you trade and what you have the EA's parameters set to. I would test at .1 lots if you are trading a number of pairs.

are my observaton about the EA

is 95 % ok  On JPY/us$

Other pairs are not performing to my expectation

Fast EMA  original  18  changed to  5

Slow EMA original   24  Changed to 10

DivergenceLimit     .0002 changed to .0005

The above changes are made duing my back testing process and  I have found  the number of loss has reduced after the change in the settings

My other observations are

Avoid EA during news time

Avoid EA during market change over like Japan to UK& Europe ad the last part

of US market

Hi guys,

This is my first post on FF, although I’ve been lurking on FF forum for about a year, I see that this thread is freezing, so I just wanted to share my thought hoping for good feedbacks from all you guys. So here’s my thought,

I’m busy doing my job since I’m an employee, so I wanted to have a minimum control of my chart, I just want a daily control, secondly there is no EA that works forever since the market is changing overtime so I have to “drive” the EA manually ( set the EA “Long only” or “Short only”), I’ll show you how.

1. Put the EA on 5 Min chart
2. Put the template and indicator on your daily chart

How to start and “drive” the EA
1. See the trend on daily chart just like the pic below,
2. When you see the trend down on daily chart, “Drive” the EA “Short only” on your 5 min chart, and vice versa
3. When you see the trend is changing on daily chart then you have to “drive” your EA on 5 min chart accordingly

Maybe theres a question, if you see the trend is clear so why you have to use this EA? My experience is that this EA can catch pips more than the market pip range , for example from January 1st Jan to January 7th the price move down for 500 pips, then this EA can catch more than 500 pips from the price retracement, just try this EA on back test for 1 month on Aug 2008 you will see that.

Less stress because you don’t trade news and not sit in front of your computer for a long time, just check it once a day.

I used GBPUSD and EURUSD or you can try another pair, just look for the pair that shows a clear trend in mid or long term

Default setting for the EA is set to 5 digit broker platform, you can change it, and also the TP and pipstep as you feel comfort.

I know there’s gotta be a negative side from this “EA drive” thing, I know some but I prefer to hear the feedback from you guys.

English is not my default language, so…sory for my bad English.

Samurai Power

--- 帖子 #2105 ---
usually 20 open position at the same time is not normal, maybe u should check the setting for the pipstep.

lets me show u this,the default setting for pipstep is 40 pips, then when u open buy position and then the market goes against u for -40pips, then the ea will open another buy position, it will do the same thing when it touch -80pips and so on. so check your pipstep and adjust it to your broker platform, the default is for 5 digit broker platform.

so according to SL for 300 and pipstep is 40 then maximum open position at a time is 300 devide by 40 is 7 maximum open position at a time.

regards

Guys,

I think there is no EA that will generate profit last forever since the market is changing overtime.

"EA IS TO MAKE YOUR TRADE EASIER, NOT TO MAKE YOUR LIFE EASIER",

so dont put all of your life on it.

Here is my illustration,

let say you set your EA to open position when the market form this condition

(I ilustrate the market condition = sequence of numbers, just like below)

5-4-6-8-9....

when this sequence of numbers forms, the EA will open position and expected to be profit next, let say at this present this market condition generate 80% profit and 20% loss, and you happy

but the market is changing soon or later, and this sequence of numbers no longer profitting, and you pee in your pants.

I think the goal is how to make profit with minimum control and less stress,

even the best strategy like 4H MACD from Phillip Nell is not 100% win, still need brain to manage money management, but with 70% probability of winning the trade.

the basic of my firebird setting (see post 2090) is no different with 4H MACD P. Nell, you still need to:

manage money management,

look for a good entry setup condition,

stay away from the unpredictable, market,

and bla...bla...

the only different is that there is one hard part from the trade that automated (so I use this EA), I say hard becouse I still pee on my pants when I open position and the market against me (can't control my emotion he...).

so "DRIVE" the EA and enter the trade when the market shows a good entry setup, that's how to avoid a huge drawdown.

any other suggestion? or any demo result to post?

regards,

HI jdogg4000,

It depends to the market,I usually look for the daily candle pattern as my other indicator, but when the market is about to change I close all the opening position of course. This is what I do when I notice that the market is about to change:

1. Safe way, not trade when the market is in the midle of changing direction, and continue to ride the market when the trend is clear, this avoiding drawdown, just take 7 days trading in a month and you probably got 1000pips. Strongly recomended to use this way.

2 Still trading when the market is about to change, I use this just to confirm when the market is about to changing, when I see the frofit for the day less than 100 pips or even negative (but often still profit but minimum) that means I have to Drive the EA accordingly.  But I dont recomend this, I only use this way on the demo.

Hope that help jdogg4000

Without reading the whole thread (I know I should), it seems this EA is a lot like it, except you are using it only for either a long or short position based on your reading of what the daily trend is. But, isn't the issue the RETRACE and not the trend? Let's say you buy or sell the EURO, because your chart says it's trending long and it steadily climbs up 300 points, and the biggest retrace was 25 pips in that whole move. You already have several positions at increasing lot sizes, so you really can't buy anymore. Because the pair is now 125 PIPS above your last trade, you need a retrace of 80 PIPS to close all trades either even or in profit. What if it never does? What if it just keeps trending up another 400 points? That's my main concern.

I just came across this thread the other day, and see this EA has been around for awhile, and a lot of people were gung ho about it, and apparently got killed in a heavily trending market when the pair(s) just kept going up or down. There hasn't been much posting sine about September of last year.

I've put it on 4 pairs just to see how it works. Samur, I admire your statements and that you've been able to get 100 pips consistently.

On IBFX, the standard setting of.10 is ten cents. On a $3,000 account, that's good to start with. I like your idea of going with the current trend only. I suppose if you're in a trade such as the GBP, and the trend changes overnight, you can always just close that trade and go the other way. When I look back at the first post here, I see very low take profits and pipsteps. I gather someone decided those should be changed, because the v63 EA has default settings of MUCH higher pips.

Does anyone know these were changed? Was it to eliminate too many trades?

In future posts, I'll talk about an EA created by a guy named nanningbob that is very similar, and a new concept of opening trades at extremes when the pair exceeds it's 40 Moving Average by 80, 90, 100, 120 pips (whatever you want to set it at). This goes against the trend, and opens additional trades at whatever distance you want. It's the opposite of this EA. It's a counter trend EA.

I don't see how people got busted using this EA. If you use a stop of 300 pips, you can simply calculate how much % of your account that is, and set the EA to trade only the amount of lots that would equal 2-3% of your account if you were stopped out.

One of the threads nanningbob has posts on is "100X80 EA oh boy" for anyone that is interested.

--- 帖子 #2150 ---
I've been trying this EA also, and had it set for LONG on the EUR/USD and had trades opened. Then, the trend changed. The question is at what point do you close out these losing trades? Do you hold them & hope the trend will change back the next day? At what point do you look at the trend? New York session? Tokoyo? London? If you don't close out trades, and the trend reverses, you can have quite a few trades open that would each lose 300 PIPS. Haven't given up on this EA yet, though.

Why is it used like it is where it opens additional trades, each subject to a 300 PIP loss? Has anyone ever tried it with 50 TP and a 150 Stop Loss? I think this is probably why people lost interest in this EA. The possibility and even PROBABILITY of huge losses when th etrend changes and you don't know whether the trend may come back to you, or not. In the meantime, you're stuck with trades that each hit a 300 PIP stop loss.

good point iopoipoi,

Here is what I mean with clear trend

Clear down trend

when the chart turns red and the arrow pointing down and the candle pattern confirm it ( I suggest U to learn candle pattern, I got this suggestion from Phillip Nell with his great 4H MACD strategy), thats where the high probability of the next daily candle move down. if one of this indis is not in the line it means that u have to becareful, or much better not to trade, trade 7 days a month is enough to have "maybe" arround 1000pips.

U can use your own indis as u feel comfort iopoipoi.

Clear up trend

vice versa

--- 帖子 #2181 ---
The attached indicator is to help those who have been looking for a single and simple way of knowing the trend across all timeframes. Even by operating on a 1min chart, you'll be able to quickly figure out whether the 4hr and Daily charts are trending up/down so as to launch the Firebird EA in the right direction. Same applies to when the trend is beginning to change.

--- 帖子 #2195 ---
I have been Strategy Testing a program unrelated to Firebird that increases/decreases lot size based on % of changing account balances. Good idea but hard to administer. Get the lot size a little too large and margin out. Take a loss when the account balance/lot size is large and loose nine months of gain. Double ouch.

The solution? Not sure. Be very conservative with the percent of lot size changes? Drain off profits all along the way, (best choice of the two) in which case the account balance does not get dangeriously high?

A great and reasonably priced, (Euros) fast programing service that did my code was Witold Wosniak at vitovd@gmail.com. Witold is in Poland and has perfect English and amazing knowledge of Expert Advisors. He is a rare find and will help you endlessly as you progress in experience. Good luck in your trading.

Not much sense in taking a poll.  The firebird is legendary.  It has been around for a long time, and many many people have tried to make it work.  EVERYONE WISHES it would work, since the concept is so elegant and very profitable when things are right.

One thing for sure,  Left to its own devices, it will make you rich, and then make you poor even quicker.

I know a few guys who have done just fine with it, by intervening a managing it,  turning it on only when market conditions are right, turning it on only on certain times of day.  I hope someday, someone is able to make it work.

Look for the "Driving the firebird" thread.  It may have had the best success so far.  It's an old thread, and I don't know how active it is.
